            <h1>Man roasts a LIVE puppy over a fire 'so he can eat the dog's meat' in sickening video filmed by his colleague</h1>      
      <ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class=""><strong>WARNING: DISTURBING CONTENT </strong></li><li class=""><strong>The man, in China, admitted to killing the dog in his factory complex yesterday</strong></li><li class=""><strong>His colleague filmed him doing so before posting the video online to show off </strong></li><li class=""><strong>The man said he likes eating dogs and had killed two canines, a source claimed</strong></li><li class=""><strong>Dog owners tracked him down and went to challenge him after seeing the video</strong></li><li class=""><strong>PETA Asia urged the Chinese authority to pass animal protection law  </strong></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By

<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Tracy+You" class="author" rel="nofollow">Tracy You</a>


and 
<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Tiffany+Lo+For+Mailonline" class="author" rel="nofollow">Tiffany Lo For Mailonline</a>

</p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font">A man in <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" href="/news/china/index.html" id="mol-67d52b70-b4c5-11e7-b5d3-fd7eef23a883">China</a> yesterday roasted a live puppy over a fire  so he could enjoy the dog's meat, animal lovers have told MailOnline.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The man's sickening behaviour was filmed by one of his colleagues who later shared the clip to their friends on social media as a show-off, a Jiujiang-based animal lover claimed.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The animal lover added that the man later showed her the dog's remains, which had been decapitated by him.</p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group"><div class="splitLeft"><div class="mol-img">      <div class="image-wrap">

      </div>

    </noscript>

</div></div><div class="splitRight"><div class="mol-img">      <div class="image-wrap">
        <img id="i-6bcc225737f53cc" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/10/19/12/457D241400000578-4996818-image-a-13_1508413596943.jpg" height="490" width="306" alt="He held the screaming animal by a string around its neck over a fire in a factory complex" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
      </div>

    <img id="i-6bcc225737f53cc" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/10/19/12/457D241400000578-4996818-image-a-13_1508413596943.jpg" height="490" width="306" alt="He held the screaming animal by a string around its neck over a fire in a factory complex" class="blkBorder img-share"/>

</div><p class="mol-para-with-font">The animal lover has agreed to be identified only by her surname Jin, due to safety concerns.  </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Ms Jin is the leader of an online animal group in Jiujiang, which is a city of around 44 million residents in Jiangxi Province.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Ms Jin said she was sent the video by a friend at around 2:20pm on October 18 through WeChat, a popular chatting app in China.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">She was told that the video had been widely shared on WeChat.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">In the video, the factory worker held the puppy over a fire by a string around its neck. The puppy was struggling and screaming at the beginning, but remained motionless in the end.  </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The video was supplied to MailOnline by PETA Asia, an animal welfare organisation. MailOnline has decided not to show the footage due to its graphic nature. </p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group"><div class="splitLeft"><div class="mol-img">      <div class="image-wrap">
        <img id="i-4747da704b4981a5" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/10/19/12/457DDAE300000578-4996818-image-a-22_1508413700445.jpg" height="444" width="306" alt="After watching the video, animal lovers managed to find the man and challenged his behaviour" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
      </div>
    <noscript>

    <img id="i-4747da704b4981a5" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/10/19/12/457DDAE300000578-4996818-image-a-22_1508413700445.jpg" height="444" width="306" alt="After watching the video, animal lovers managed to find the man and challenged his behaviour" class="blkBorder img-share"/>

    </noscript>

</div></div><div class="splitRight"><div class="mol-img">      <div class="image-wrap">
        <img id="i-ebceabab3845f27c" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/10/19/12/457DDA4F00000578-4996818-image-a-23_1508413703467.jpg" height="444" width="306" alt="Footage provided by Ms Jin, an animal lover, shows them talking to the man" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
      </div>
    <noscript>

    <img id="i-ebceabab3845f27c" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/10/19/12/457DDA4F00000578-4996818-image-a-23_1508413703467.jpg" height="444" width="306" alt="Footage provided by Ms Jin, an animal lover, shows them talking to the man" class="blkBorder img-share"/>

    </noscript>

</div></div><div class="clear"></div><p class="imageCaption">After watching the video, animal lovers managed to find the man and challenged his behaviour. Footage provided by Ms Jin, an animal lover, shows them talking to the man</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font">Ms Jin said after she saw the video, she decided to find the man and tell him what he had done was wrong. The animal lover, who owns a Labrador, went out  with 10 other dog owners in hope of finding the man.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">As the post claimed the man was a worker at the Jiujiang Power Supply Station, Ms Jin showed the video to people around the station to ask if they had seen him. Ms Jin said she eventually found the man in the power station at around 4:10pm.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">After Ms Jin and the other animal lovers challenged the man and his colleagues, the man admitted that he had burnt the puppy because he liked eating dog meat, according to Ms Jin.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Ms Jin also said this was the second time the man had killed a dog in this way, as he told the animal lovers.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Then he showed the animal lovers the remains of the animal  in a bucket, which was said to have been decapitated.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">It's said that the man had apologised for his behaviour to the animal lovers orally, and promised not to do it again. He said he would issue them a promise letter to show them his determination.</p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">      <div class="image-wrap">
        <img id="i-9ed34bfe3cc461ed" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/10/19/12/457CCF1900000578-4996818-image-a-24_1508413717026.jpg" height="475" width="634" alt="The incident is said to take place in Jiujiang (pictured), a city of 44 million residents in China" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
      </div>
    <noscript>

    <img id="i-9ed34bfe3cc461ed" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2017/10/19/12/457CCF1900000578-4996818-image-a-24_1508413717026.jpg" height="475" width="634" alt="The incident is said to take place in Jiujiang (pictured), a city of 44 million residents in China" class="blkBorder img-share"/>

    </noscript>

</div>    <p class="imageCaption">The incident is said to take place in Jiujiang (pictured), a city of 44 million residents in China</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font">During the conversation, physical clashes were said to have occurred between the animal lovers and the man's colleague. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Police from the Changhong Police station reportedly arrived at the scene and brought the two parties back to the station for questioning. Both parties were released by the police in the evening, said Ms Jin. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The man who killed the puppy remained at large, as it's understood. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">PETA Asia told MailOnline that because there is a lack of animal protection law in China, people who are suspected of abusing them would not be arrested and could not be subjected to the legal punishment.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The group said at the moment China only has law for protecting wild animals, but no law for protecting livestock and small animals, such as dogs and cats.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Jason Baker, PETA Asia Vice President, said: 'We hope that someone at the 19th National Congress of Commuist Party might see this and call for a law to be passed today.' </p><p class="mol-para-with-font"></p></div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 0;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n,
                target_type: 'mix'
            });
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=news&pageSize=10',
            total: 16.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
